Important: Do not remove the memory card when an app is using it. Doing so may damage the memory card and the device and corrupt data stored on the card. Remove the memory card Open the back cover, and push the memory card in until it's released. Switch your phone on Press and hold the power key.. Lock Unlock the keypad Press , and select Unlock. Set which SIM card to use If you have 2 SIM cards in your phone, you can select which one you want to use. Select Menu > Settings > Connectivity > Dual SIM. Comfortable display Powerful battery Convenient design Reasonably priced. Looking for a cool and stylish dual SIM handset that does not ask you to spend much? Well, the Nokia 225 Dual is the latest addition to this market in this regard. It comes with the reliability and durability of Nokia and offers a host of smart and attractive features. You can choose from a number of eye catching colors which include yellow, white, red, green and black.. The Nokia 225 Dual has been featured with a 2.8-inch LCD Transmissive display equipped with 256K colors, a QVGA resolution of 240 x 320 pixels and a pixel density of 143ppi. It runs Nokia Series 30+ OS out of the box.. The handset has been crafted in a manner that it can be easily carried around almost anywhere you go. The splash and dust proof keymat makes the handset withstand tough circumstances. Being 10.4mm thick, it can be easily rated as one of the slimmest low priced handsets with internet connectivity.. A 2MP camera on the rear panel of the Nokia 225 Dual enables you to capture quality photos and videos and share them instantly without any additional formatting. It has a resolution of 1,600 x 1,200 pixels and records QVGA videos at the rate of 15fps. The handset is capable of supporting up to 32GB of microSD cards so that the user never runs short of memory while loading apps, games, music, videos and images.. The Nokia 225 Dual justifies of the manufacturer in delivering an uninterrupted service for a long time. With the 1,200mAh BL-4U, it can render up to 648 hours of standby life, up to 21 hours of talktime and up to 49 hours of music playback time.. The handset comes preloaded with all the popular social networking apps so that you can stay close to your friend and share photos and videos on the move. Enjoy seamless and economical internet connectivity with the Xpress Browser loaded with Bing search option. And with the Dual SIM cards functioned to operate in a smarter way, you can set up both forwarding and waiting options between the two SIMs.. To summarize, connectivity options include Bluetooth 3.0, USB port and GPRS with EDGE.. Nokia 225 Dual SIM PRICE IN INDIA. Nokia 225 Dual SIM price in India starts from Rs. Nokia 225 and 225 Dual SIM, Internet-Enabled Feature Phones Announced. Published: Wednesday, April 9, 2014, 17:23 [IST]. Finnish smartphone maker Nokia has today launched its latest internet enabled feature phones called the Nokia 225 and 225 Dual SIM at a price of 39 Euros (approx. The Nokia 225 and 225 Dual SIM would be available in red, yellow, green, black and white colors priced at without taxes. Both these models will go on sale in select markets globally in Q2 2014.. The device is very similar to company's C1 and C2 devices which are basic feature-phones. In terms of specs and features Nokia 225 and 225 Dual SIM, are the company's most affordable internet-enabled handsets. The Nokia 225 and the 225 Dual SIM have a 2.8-inch with a QVGA resolution of 320 x 240 pixels. It comes with an LCD panel, dust and splash proof keymat, Nokia Xpress Browser, FM Radio, up to 103 phon output with Donau speaker, Bluetooth 3.0 with Slam sharing feature and a 2-megapixel fixed focus rear camera without flash. These are just 10.4mm thick and have a curved design.. Nokia Lumia 930 Vs Apple iPhone 5s: The Big Indian Market Adventure Continues. The best part of the handsets are that they both come with an ample number of pre-loaded games and apps which include social networking sites like Facebook and Twitter. Games include Block Breaker 3, Asphalt 6, Assassins Creed 3, The Avengers and Real Football 2012 games.. Top 10 Latest LG Smartphones You Could Buy In India This April. <center><iframe width="100%" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/aSqSeytngW0?feature=player_embedded" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe></center>. These run on Series 30+ OS and also supports micro SD cards up to 32GB. Both these have 1200mAh battery that promises up to 21h talk time. It would offer up to 36 days standby in the Single SIM variant and up to 27 days standby in the dual SIM variant.. "Our slimmest Internet phone to date, it also features a larger 2.8" display making it not only an ideal fit for pockets and handbags, but for also keeping you entertained on the move," a recent post on Nokia Conversations reads.. Nokia 225 Dual SIM Price in India :. - Nokia´s design and quality extend to even the most affordable handsets in our portfolio and the Nokia 225 is no exception. Our slimmest Internet phone to date, it also features a larger 2.8" display making it not only an ideal fit for pockets and handbags, but for also keeping you entertained on the move. Built to last, the Nokia 225 features a dust and splash proof keymat, and with standby times of up to 36 days for single SIM and 27 days for Dual SIM, you can stay entertained for longer. Available in five bold colours - red, yellow, green, black and white - it really stands out from the crowd. Browsing on a budget Preloaded with Nokia´s Xpress Browser, your Internet browsing data costs are kept to an absolute minimum as website data is optimised before it reaches your device, meaning all you´re left with is faster browsing speeds and lower data costs. Stay connected with friends and family with the pre-loaded Facebook and Twitter apps available direct on your homescreen, or discover the world for less with Bing search.. - We all like to take photos with our phones and the Nokia 225 offers a 2MP camera that´s perfect for the job, producing images at the ideal size for sharing on your Facebook and Twitter feeds. If you don´t want to share your images online, there´s the option to share your photos via Bluetooth to nearby friends using SLAM.. - The Nokia 225 offers a wealth of entertainment, enhanced by its larger 2.8" display. Download and play online video, listen to the built-in FM radio, or if you´d rather not wait for your favourite song to play, you can also use the Nokia 225 as an MP3 player with playback time of up to 51 hours. When you´re tired from dancing, singing or browsing, the five pre-loaded games; Block Breaker 3, Asphalt 6, Assassins Creed 3, The Avengers and Real Football 2012, can give you some well-earned downtime. With MicroSD support of up to 32GB, there is plenty of room for apps, games, music and photos. Dual SIM If you´re one of the millions out there with multiple SIM cards for work, home, data or international dialing, carrying more than one phone around with you isn´t ideal. The Nokia 225 Dual SIM may be the perfect solution allowing two different contracts to be used in one device. With an estimated retail price excluding taxes and subsidies of EUR 39, the Nokia 225 may be light on the pocket, but not on features.
